## Current operating rule
- Protected CTA analytics guard: the repeated `AI สร้างภาพสินค้า แค่ 10 บาท / ไม่ต้อง prompt` line is Sway-added CTA only. Current best/winning labels must use `educational_signal` or CTA-stripped body. Post `7634027210248097042` is evidence for ChatGPT 8 productivity tips, not product-photo/10-baht/no-prompt CTA performance.
- Sway publishes manually.
- Aion/Hermes does draft-only analytics, experiment creation, issue detection, memory logging, and self-improvement toward the KPI.
- Every recurring run should create a useful action, fix, rule update, or experiment — not only summarize.
- Education comes first; GenLabs promotion is selective. Use the final banner as the baseline CTA, and explicitly integrate `genlabs.in.th` when the topic naturally fits GenLabs software such as same-day product-photo posts, SME utility visuals, image generation, product photos, brand graphics, promo visuals, menus, posters, thumbnails, or other visual assets. Position GenLabs as the no-prompt shortcut: users focus on uploading/providing the product, and GenLabs handles the visual generation.
